+a personalized user experience and personalized content and activate your
+after-sale services.</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:Roboto;

+lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Roboto;color:gray'>&nbsp;</span></p>

+<p class=MsoListParagraph align=left style='margin-left:21.0pt;text-align:left;

+</span></span><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:Roboto;color:gray'>Improve

+
+<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='text-align:left;line-height:2.0pt'><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Roboto;color:gray'>&nbsp;</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoListParagraph align=left style='margin-left:21.0pt;text-align:left;

+Roboto;color:gray'>(h)<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
+</span></span><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:Roboto;color:gray'>Troubleshoot
+errors should you choose to send us error details.</span><span lang=EN-US

+<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='text-align:left;line-height:2.0pt'><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Roboto;color:gray'>&nbsp;</span></p>

+<p class=MsoListParagraph align=left style='margin-left:21.0pt;text-align:left;

+</span></span><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:Roboto;color:gray'>Synchronize,

+<p class=MsoListParagraph align=left style='margin-left:21.0pt;text-align:left;
+text-indent:-21.0pt;line-height:20.0pt'><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:
+Roboto;color:gray'>(j)<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
+</span></span><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:Roboto;color:gray'>Improve our
+loss prevention and anti-fraud programs.</span><span lang=EN-US
+style='font-family:Roboto;color:gray'>&nbsp;</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='text-align:left;line-height:10.0pt'><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Roboto;color:gray'>&nbsp;</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoListParagraph align=left style='margin-left:20.25pt;text-align:
+left;text-indent:-20.25pt;line-height:20.0pt'><span lang=EN-US
+style='font-family:Roboto'>1.3<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
+</span></span><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:Roboto'>Location-based
+services</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='text-align:left;line-height:2.0pt'><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-family:Roboto'>&nbsp;</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='text-align:left;line-height:20.0pt'><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-family:Roboto;color:gray'>When you access certain
+location-based services, for example, when you perform a search, use navigation
+software or check the weather for a specific location, GOME may collect, use
+and process your device's precise or fuzzy location. This is necessary for GOME
+to provide the aforementioned services. GOME may collect your device
+identification numbers (IMEI, ESN, MEID, and SN), device type, model and
+real-time location data (obtained through GPS, Wi-Fi and your service
+provider's network ID). GOME collects location data to provide and improve its
+location-based products and services.</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:
+Roboto;color:gray'>&nbsp;</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='text-align:left;line-height:2.0pt'><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Roboto;color:gray'>&nbsp;</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='text-align:left;line-height:20.0pt'><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-family:Roboto;color:gray'>We may ask you which
+applications you want location-based services to be enabled for. You can choose
+not to share your location data by turning off location-based services on your
+devices. For detailed information on how to disable location-based services,
+please contact your network operator.</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:
+Roboto;color:gray'>&nbsp;</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='text-align:left;line-height:10.0pt'><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Roboto;color:gray'>&nbsp;</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoListParagraph align=left style='margin-left:20.25pt;text-align:
+left;text-indent:-20.25pt;line-height:20.0pt'><span lang=EN-US
+style='font-family:Roboto'>1.4<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
+</span></span><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:Roboto'>Collection and use of
+non-identifiable data</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='text-align:left;line-height:2.0pt'><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Roboto'>&nbsp;</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='text-align:left;line-height:20.0pt'><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-family:Roboto;color:gray'>Non-identifiable data refers
+to data that cannot be used to identify an individual. For example, GOME may
+collect aggregated statistics, such as the number of visitors to its website.
+GOME collects this data to understand how people use its website, products and
+services. This allows GOME to improve its services to better satisfy customer
+needs. GOME may, at its own discretion, collect, use, process, transfer or
+disclose non-identifiable data for other purposes.</span><span lang=EN-US
+style='font-family:Roboto;color:gray'>&nbsp;</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='text-align:left;line-height:20.0pt'><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-family:Roboto;color:gray'>We endeavour to keep your
+personal data and non-identifiable data separate, and use each independently.
+If personal data is combined with non-identifiable data, it will be treated as
+personal data.</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:Roboto;color:gray'>&nbsp;</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='text-align:left;line-height:20.0pt'><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Roboto;color:gray'>&nbsp;</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoListParagraph align=left style='margin-left:18.0pt;text-align:left;
+text-indent:-18.0pt;line-height:20.0pt'><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
+font-family:Roboto'>2.<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
+</span></span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Roboto'>How
+GOME uses cookies and similar technologies</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='text-align:left;line-height:10.0pt'><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Roboto'>&nbsp;</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoListParagraph align=left style='margin-left:20.25pt;text-align:
+left;text-indent:-20.25pt;line-height:20.0pt'><span lang=EN-US
+style='font-family:Roboto'>2.1<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
+</span></span><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:Roboto'>Cookies</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='text-align:left;line-height:2.0pt'><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Roboto'>&nbsp;</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='text-align:left;line-height:20.0pt'><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-family:Roboto;color:gray'>To ensure that our websites
+function properly, we sometimes store small data files known as cookies on
+computers or mobile devices. A cookie is a simple text file that is stored on
+your computer or mobile device by a web server. Only the server that creates
+the cookie can retrieve or read the cookie's contents. Each cookie is unique to
+your web browser or mobile application. Cookies usually contain an identifier,
+the site name and some numbers and characters. Cookies allow websites to store
+data, such as your user preferences or the contents of your shopping basket.</span><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-family:Roboto;color:gray'>&nbsp;</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='text-align:left;line-height:2.0pt'><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Roboto;color:gray'>&nbsp;</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='text-align:left;line-height:20.0pt'><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-family:Roboto;color:gray'>Most large websites or
+Internet service providers enable cookies in order to improve their user
+experience. Cookies allow websites to remember users, either for a single visit
+(using a session cookie) or for repeated visits (using a persistent cookie). Cookies
+allow websites to store settings, such as language, font size and other viewing
+preferences for your computers or mobile devices. This means that user
+preferences do not need to be re-configured on each visit. If a website doesn't
+use cookies, it will treat its users as new visitors each time they open a
+page. For example, if you log in on a website and move to another page, the
+website won't recognize you, and you will be logged out again.</span><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-family:Roboto;color:gray'>&nbsp;</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='text-align:left;line-height:2.0pt'><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Roboto;color:gray'>&nbsp;</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='text-align:left;line-height:20.0pt'><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-family:Roboto;color:gray'>GOME does not use cookies for
+any purposes other than those specified in this Policy. You can manage or
+delete cookies according to your preferences. For more information, see http://AboutCookies.org/</span><span lang=EN-US
+style='font-family:Roboto;color:gray'>. You can clear all cookies stored on
+your computer and most web browsers can be configured to block cookies.
+However, if you do so, you may have to manually your user settings every time
+you visit our websites. For more information on how to change your browser
+settings, please visit the following links: Internet Explorer��Mozilla Firefox��Safari��Opera��</span><span lang=EN-US
+style='font-family:Roboto;color:gray'>&nbsp;</span></p>
+
+
+
+<p class=MsoListParagraph align=left style='margin-left:20.25pt;text-align:
+left;text-indent:-20.25pt;line-height:20.0pt'><span lang=EN-US
+style='font-family:Roboto'>2.2<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
+</span></span><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:Roboto'>Web beacons and pixel
+tags</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='text-align:left;line-height:2.0pt'><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Roboto'>&nbsp;</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='text-align:left;line-height:20.0pt'><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-family:Roboto;color:gray'>In addition to cookies, we
+also use other similar technologies such as web beacons and pixel tags on our
+websites. For example, when you receive an email from GOME, it may contain a
+click-through URL which links to content on GOME's website. If you click the
+link, the click-through is tracked by GOME to help us learn about your product
+and service preferences and improve our customer service. A web beacon is
+typically a transparent image that is embedded on a website or in an email. The
+inclusion of pixel tags in emails allows us to know if our emails have been
+opened. If you do not want your activities to be tracked in such a way, you may
+unsubscribe from GOME mailing lists at any time.</span><span lang=EN-US
+style='font-family:Roboto;color:gray'>&nbsp;</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='text-align:left;line-height:10.0pt'><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Roboto;color:gray'>&nbsp;</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoListParagraph align=left style='margin-left:20.25pt;text-align:
+left;text-indent:-20.25pt;line-height:20.0pt'><span lang=EN-US
+style='font-family:Roboto'>2.3<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
+</span></span><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:Roboto'>Do Not Track</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='text-align:left;line-height:2.0pt'><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Roboto'>&nbsp;</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='text-align:left;line-height:20.0pt'><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-family:Roboto;color:gray'>Many web browsers have a Do
+Not Track feature, which issues Do Not Track requests to websites. Currently,
+the main Internet standards organization has no policy governing how websites
+should behave when they receive such requests. However, all GOME websites do
+respect the Do Not Track </span><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-family:Roboto;color:gray'> option if it is enabled in
+your browser.</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:Roboto;color:gray'>&nbsp;</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='text-align:left;line-height:20.0pt'><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Roboto;color:gray'>&nbsp;</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoListParagraph align=left style='margin-left:18.0pt;text-align:left;
+text-indent:-18.0pt;line-height:20.0pt'><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
+font-family:Roboto'>3.<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
+</span></span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Roboto'>How
+GOME discloses your personal data</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='text-align:left;line-height:10.0pt'><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Roboto'>&nbsp;</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='text-align:left;line-height:20.0pt'><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-family:Roboto;color:gray'>GOME does not sell your
+personal data to third parties. However, GOME may disclose your personal data
+under the following circumstances:</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:
+Roboto;color:gray'>&nbsp;</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='text-align:left;line-height:10.0pt'><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Roboto'>&nbsp;</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoListParagraph align=left style='margin-left:20.25pt;text-align:
+left;text-indent:-20.25pt;line-height:20.0pt'><span lang=EN-US
+style='font-family:Roboto'>3.1<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
+</span></span><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:Roboto'>Disclosures with
+explicit consent: </span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoListParagraph align=left style='margin-left:20.25pt;text-align:
+left;text-indent:0cm;line-height:20.0pt'><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:
+Roboto;color:gray'>After obtaining your explicit approval, GOME may share your
+personal data with other parties.</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:
+Roboto;color:gray'>&nbsp;</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='text-align:left;line-height:10.0pt'><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Roboto;color:gray'>&nbsp;</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoListParagraph align=left style='margin-left:20.25pt;text-align:
+left;text-indent:-20.25pt;line-height:20.0pt'><span lang=EN-US
+style='font-family:Roboto'>3.2<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
+</span></span><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:Roboto'>Disclosures to GOME
+affiliates: </span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoListParagraph align=left style='margin-left:20.25pt;text-align:
+left;text-indent:0cm;line-height:20.0pt'><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:
+Roboto;color:gray'>Your personal data may be shared with GOME's affiliates. As
+a matter of policy, we will only disclose data that is necessary.</span><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-family:Roboto;color:gray'>&nbsp;</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='text-align:left;line-height:10.0pt'><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Roboto'>&nbsp;</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoListParagraph align=left style='margin-left:20.25pt;text-align:
+left;text-indent:-20.25pt;line-height:20.0pt'><span lang=EN-US
+style='font-family:Roboto'>3.3<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
+</span></span><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:Roboto'>Disclosures to
+authorized partners (&quot;our Partners&quot;): </span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoListParagraph align=left style='margin-left:20.25pt;text-align:
+left;text-indent:0cm;line-height:20.0pt'><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:
+Roboto;color:gray'>Some GOME services are provided by our Partners. GOME may
+share some of your personal data with its Partners to offer better customer
+service and an improved user experience. For example, when you purchase GOME
+products online, GOME must share your personal data with logistics providers to
+schedule a delivery, or arrange for Partners to provide services. Your personal
+data may only be processed for specified, explicit and legitimate purposes, and
+only the data that is necessary to offer a service shall be disclosed. GOME
+subsidiaries or Partners are not authorized to use shared personal data for any
+other purpose.</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:Roboto;color:gray'>&nbsp;</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='text-align:left;line-height:10.0pt'><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Roboto;color:gray'>&nbsp;</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoListParagraph align=left style='margin-left:20.25pt;text-align:
+left;text-indent:-20.25pt;line-height:20.0pt'><span lang=EN-US
+style='font-family:Roboto'>3.4<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
+</span></span><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:Roboto'>Disclosures on legal
+or reasonable grounds: </span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoListParagraph align=left style='margin-left:20.25pt;text-align:
+left;text-indent:0cm;line-height:20.0pt'><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:
+Roboto;color:gray'>GOME may disclose your personal data if required by the law,
+legal proceedings, litigation or public and governmental authorities. In some
+jurisdictions, your personal data may also be disclosed to transaction parties
+if GOME is involved in a reorganization, merger or insolvency and liquidation
+proceedings. GOME may also disclose your data where reasonable need can be
+demonstrated, such as to enforce its terms and conditions and to protect its
+customers.</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:Roboto;color:gray'>&nbsp;</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='text-align:left;line-height:20.0pt'><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Roboto;color:gray'>&nbsp;</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='text-align:left;line-height:20.0pt'><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Roboto'>4. How to access or
+modify your personal data</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='text-align:left;line-height:10.0pt'><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Roboto'>&nbsp;</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='text-align:left;line-height:20.0pt'><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-family:Roboto;color:gray'>Under GOME's terms and
+conditions, you can manage your personal data, such as your account
+information, at any time. You should ensure that all personal data submitted is
+accurate. GOME will make reasonable efforts to keep your personal data
+accurate, complete and up-to-date.&nbsp;</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='text-align:left;line-height:2.0pt'><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-family:Roboto;color:gray'>&nbsp;</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='text-align:left;line-height:20.0pt'><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-family:Roboto;color:gray'>You have a right to access
+your personal data, subject to some legal exceptions. Where privacy and
+information laws differ in some jurisdictions, we will comply with them. If you
+would like to exercise your right to access data, please contact us by </span><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-family:Roboto;color:gray'>400-898-8666</span><span
+style='font-family:������ͤ��_GBK;color:gray'>��</span><span lang=EN-US
+style='font-family:Roboto;color:gray'>&nbsp;. For security reasons, you may be
+required to put your request in writing.&nbsp;</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='text-align:left;line-height:2.0pt'><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-family:Roboto;color:gray'>&nbsp;</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='text-align:left;line-height:20.0pt'><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-family:Roboto;color:gray'>You also have the right to
+delete or amend any personal information about you that we hold. GOME will
+delete or amend such information upon your request. To make such a request, you
+can contact us by</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:Roboto;color:gray'>&nbsp;</span><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-family:Roboto;color:gray'>400-898-8666</span><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-family:Roboto;color:gray'>. We may decline to process

+faith, are impractical or if access is not otherwise required by local law.</span><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-family:Roboto;color:gray'>&nbsp;</span></p>

+<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='text-align:left;line-height:20.0pt'><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Roboto'>5. How GOME protects your
+personal data</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='text-align:left;line-height:10.0pt'><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Roboto'>&nbsp;</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='text-align:left;line-height:20.0pt'><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-family:Roboto;color:gray'>GOME takes personal data
+security seriously. We follow industry-standard practices to safeguard your
+personal data against unauthorized access, disclosure, use, modification,
+damage or loss. We take all reasonably practicable steps to protect your
+personal data. For example, we use encryption to ensure data confidentiality;
+we use trusted protection mechanisms to protect data from malicious attacks; we
+deploy visit control mechanisms to ensure only authorized personnel can access
+personal data; and we raise awareness among employees about the importance of
+protecting personal data through security and privacy protection training
+sessions.</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:Roboto;color:gray'>&nbsp;</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='text-align:left;line-height:2.0pt'><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Roboto;color:gray'>&nbsp;</span></p>

+lang=EN-US style='font-family:Roboto;color:gray'>We take all reasonably
+practicable steps to only collect relevant personal data. We only retain your
+personal data for the period necessary to fulfil the purposes outlined in this
+Policy, unless a longer retention period is required or permitted by law. While
+we take the utmost care to protect your personal data, please note that no
+security measures are completely infallible.</span><span lang=EN-US
+style='font-family:Roboto;color:gray'>&nbsp;</span></p>

+    boolean handlePinMmi(String dialString);
+    void toggleRadioOnOff();
+    boolean setRadio(boolean turnOn);
+    void updateServiceLocation();
+    void enableLocationUpdates();
+    void disableLocationUpdates();
+    int enableApnType(String type);
+    int disableApnType(String type);
+    boolean enableDataConnectivity();
+    boolean disableDataConnectivity();
+    boolean isDataConnectivityPossible();
+    Bundle getCellLocation();
+    List<NeighboringCellInfo> getNeighboringCellInfo();

+     int getDataActivity();
+     int getDataState();
+    int getActivePhoneType();
+    int getCdmaEriIconIndex();
+    int getCdmaEriIconMode();
+    String getCdmaEriText();
+    boolean getCdmaNeedsProvisioning();
+    int getVoiceMessageCount();
+    int getNetworkType();
+    boolean hasIccCard();

+import com.gome.bootwizard.receiver.SIMCardStateReceiver;
+import com.gome.bootwizard.util.HasPreferences;
+import com.gome.bootwizard.util.HasRequest;

+import android.view.View.OnClickListener;

+/**
+ * SIM Card page
+ *
+ * @author Yusong.Liang
+ * @date 2017/5/10.
+ */
+public class SIMCardActivity extends BaseActivity implements HasRequest,HasPreferences,OnClickListener,
+        SIMCardStateReceiver.OnSIMCardStateChangeListener {
+
+    private SIMCardStateReceiver mReceiver;
+    private IntentFilter mFilter;
+	BottomActionBar mBottomActionBar;
+    @Override
+    protected int getLayoutResID() {
+        return R.layout.activity_sim_card;
+    }
+
+    @Override
+    protected void onResume() {
+        super.onResume();
+        if (mFilter == null) {
+            mFilter = new IntentFilter(SIMCardStateReceiver.ACTION_SIM_STATE_CHANGED);
+            mFilter.setPriority(IntentFilter.SYSTEM_HIGH_PRIORITY);
+        }
+        if (mReceiver == null) {
+            mReceiver = new SIMCardStateReceiver();
+        }
+        Intent intentAction2 = new Intent();
+        intentAction2.setPackage("com.android.systemui");
+        intentAction2.setAction("hide_navigationbar");
+        sendBroadcast(intentAction2);
+        registerReceiver(mReceiver, mFilter);
+        mReceiver.setOnSIMCardStateChangeListener(this);
+    }
+
+    @Override
+    protected void onPause() {
+        super.onPause();
+        unregisterReceiver(mReceiver);
+    }
+
+    @Override
+    public void onSIMCardStateChange(boolean isReady) {
+        if (isReady) {
+            MoveToWlan();
+            finish();
+        }
+    }
+    private void MoveToWlan(){
+        final boolean mBooleanConnect = WifiUtils.isConnect(SIMCardActivity.this);
+        Intent intent = new Intent();
+        intent.setAction("android.net.wifi.PICK_WIFI_NETWORK");
+        intent.putExtra("extra_prefs_show_button_bar", true);
+
+        if (mBooleanConnect){
+            intent.putExtra("extra_prefs_set_next_text", getResources().getString(R.string.forward));
+        }else{
+            intent.putExtra("extra_prefs_set_next_text", getResources().getString(R.string.skip));
+        }
+        intent.putExtra("extra_prefs_set_back_text", getResources().getString(R.string.back));
+        intent.putExtra("wifi_enable_next_on_connect", true);
+        intent.putExtra("wifi_from_boot_wizard", true);
+        startActivity(intent);
+    }
+	
+	@Override
+	public void onClick(View view) {
+	// TODO Auto-generated method stub
+	switch (view.getId()) {
+            case R.id.btn_previous:
+                mNavigator.navigateToLanguageSelectActivity(this);
+                overridePendingTransition(R.anim.gome_activity_close_enter,R.anim.gome_activity_close_exit);
+                Log.e("btn_previous","btn_previous");
+                finish();
+                break;
+            case R.id.btn_next:
+                MoveToWlan();
+                overridePendingTransition(R.anim.gome_activity_open_enter,R.anim.gome_activity_open_exit);
+                Log.e("btn_next","btn_next");
+                finish();
+                break;
+            
+        }
+	}
+	/*

+    @SuppressWarnings("unchecked")
+    protected void changeSystemLanguage(LocaleList locale) {
+        if (locale != null) {
+            try {
+                Class classActivityManagerNative = Class.forName("android.app.ActivityManagerNative");
+                Method getDefault = classActivityManagerNative.getDeclaredMethod("getDefault");
+                Object objIActivityManager = getDefault.invoke(classActivityManagerNative);
+                Class classIActivityManager = Class.forName("android.app.IActivityManager");
+                Method getConfiguration = classIActivityManager.getDeclaredMethod("getConfiguration");
+                Configuration config = (Configuration) getConfiguration.invoke(objIActivityManager);
+                config.setLocales(locale);
+                Class clzConfig = Class
+                        .forName("android.content.res.Configuration");
+                java.lang.reflect.Field userSetLocale = clzConfig
+                        .getField("userSetLocale");
+                userSetLocale.set(config, true);
+                Class[] clzParams = {Configuration.class};
+                Method updateConfiguration = classIActivityManager.getDeclaredMethod("updatePersistentConfiguration", clzParams);
+                updateConfiguration.invoke(objIActivityManager, config);
+                BackupManager.dataChanged("com.android.providers.settings");
+            } catch (Exception e) {
+                Log.d(TAG, "changeSystemLanguage: " + e.getLocalizedMessage());
+            }
+        }
+    }

+package com.gome.bootwizard.activity;
+
+import android.content.Intent;
+import android.content.res.Configuration;
+import android.os.Bundle;
+import android.util.Log;
+import android.view.View;
+import android.webkit.WebResourceRequest;
+import android.webkit.WebView;
+import android.webkit.WebViewClient;
+import android.widget.ImageButton;
+
+import com.gome.bootwizard.R;
+import com.gome.bootwizard.widget.AppTitleBar;
+
+import java.util.Locale;
+
+//import butterknife.BindView;

+/**
+ * @author Yusong.Liang
+ * @date 2017/5/17.
+ */
+public class UserAgreementActivity extends BaseActivity {
+
+
+    AppTitleBar appTitleBar;
+
+    WebView webView;
+    private int mIndex;
+    @Override
+    protected int getLayoutResID() {
+        return R.layout.activity_user_agreement;
+    }
+	
+
+	
+    @Override
+    protected void initData(Bundle savedInstanceState) {
+appTitleBar = (AppTitleBar) findViewById(R.id.appTitleBar);
+//        appTitleBar.setPadding(0, getStatusBarHeight(), 0, 0);
+        Log.e("BootWizard_welcome","UserAgreementActivity");
+        mIndex = getSavedLanguage();
+        webView=(WebView) findViewById(R.id.tv_user_agreement_content);
+        webView.getSettings().setJavaScriptEnabled(true);
+        webView.setWebViewClient(new WebClient());
+        initViewState();
+        webView.setOnLongClickListener(new View.OnLongClickListener() {    @Override    public boolean onLongClick(View view) {        return true;    }});
+
+        ImageButton mImageButton = (ImageButton) findViewById(R.id.ib_title_bar_back);
+        mImageButton.setOnClickListener(new View.OnClickListener() {
+            @Override
+            public void onClick(View view) {
+                finish();
+                overridePendingTransition(R.anim.gome_activity_close_enter,R.anim.gome_activity_close_exit);
+            }
+        });
+    }
+    private int getSavedLanguage() {
+        final Configuration config = getResources().getConfiguration();
+        final Locale locale = config.locale;
+
+        if (Locale.SIMPLIFIED_CHINESE.equals(locale)) return 0;
+        else if (Locale.US.equals(locale)) return 1;
+        else return 2;
+    }
+    private void initViewState() {
+        switch (mIndex) {
+            case 1://english
+                webView.loadUrl("file:///android_asset/User_Agreement_US.html");
+                break;
+            case 0://chinese
+                webView.loadUrl("file:///android_asset/User_Agreement_CN.html");
+                break;
+            case 2:
+            default:
+                webView.loadUrl("file:///android_asset/User_Agreement_CN.html");
+
+                break;
+        }
+    }
+
+    @Override
+    protected void onResume() {
+        super.onResume();
+        Intent intentAction2 = new Intent();
+        intentAction2.setPackage("com.android.systemui");
+        intentAction2.setAction("hide_navigationbar");
+        sendBroadcast(intentAction2);
+    }
+    class WebClient extends WebViewClient {
+        @Override
+        public boolean shouldOverrideUrlLoading(WebView view, WebResourceRequest request) {
+            return true;
+        }
+    }

+package com.gome.bootwizard.activity;
+
+import android.app.Activity;
+import android.app.Application;
+import android.content.Intent;
+import android.os.Bundle;
+import android.util.Log;
+
+/**
+ * Created by Administrator on 2017/9/19.
+ */
+
+public class AndroidApplication extends Application {
+
+    private static AndroidApplication instance;
+
+    @Override
+    public void onCreate() {
+        super.onCreate();
+        instance = this;
+        Intent intentAction2 = new Intent();
+        intentAction2.setPackage("com.android.systemui");
+        intentAction2.setAction("hide_navigationbar");
+        sendBroadcast(intentAction2);
+        registerActivityLifecycleCallbacks(mCallback);
+    }
+
+    public static AndroidApplication getInstance(){
+        return instance;
+    }
+
+    private final ActivityCallback mCallback=new ActivityCallback();
+
+    private class ActivityCallback implements ActivityLifecycleCallbacks{
+
+        @Override
+        public void onActivityCreated(Activity activity, Bundle bundle) {
+            Log.e("Wizard###!!!", activity.getClass().getSimpleName()+"onActivityCreated:hashCode = "+hashCode());
+        }
+
+        @Override
+        public void onActivityStarted(Activity activity) {
+            Log.e("Wizard###!!!", activity.getClass().getSimpleName()+"onActivityStarted:hashCode = "+hashCode());
+        }
+
+        @Override
+        public void onActivityResumed(Activity activity) {
+            Log.e("Wizard###!!!", activity.getClass().getSimpleName()+"onActivityResumed:hashCode = "+hashCode());
+        }

+        window.clearFlags(WindowManager.LayoutParams.FLAG_TRANSLUCENT_STATUS
+                | WindowManager.LayoutParams.FLAG_TRANSLUCENT_NAVIGATION);
+        window.getDecorView().setSystemUiVisibility(View.SYSTEM_UI_FLAG_LAYOUT_FULLSCREEN
+                | View.SYSTEM_UI_FLAG_LAYOUT_HIDE_NAVIGATION
+                | View.SYSTEM_UI_FLAG_LAYOUT_STABLE
+                | View.SYSTEM_UI_FLAG_LIGHT_STATUS_BAR
+                | View.SYSTEM_UI_FLAG_HIDE_NAVIGATION
+                | View.SYSTEM_UI_FLAG_IMMERSIVE_STICKY
+        );
+        window.addFlags(WindowManager.LayoutParams.FLAG_DRAWS_SYSTEM_BAR_BACKGROUNDS);
+        window.setStatusBarColor(Color.TRANSPARENT);
+        window.setNavigationBarColor(Color.TRANSPARENT);
+    }

+    protected boolean willShowActivity(String extraName) {
+        final SharedPreferences preferences = getDefaultSharedPreferences();
+        return preferences == null || !preferences.getBoolean(extraName, false);
+    }

+    protected int getStatusBarHeight() {
+        int result = 0;
+        int resourceId = getResources().getIdentifier("status_bar_height", "dimen", "android");
+        if (resourceId > 0) {
+            result = getResources().getDimensionPixelSize(resourceId);
+        }
+        return result;
+    }
+    /**
+     * 隐藏虚拟按键，并且全屏
+     */
+    protected void hideBottomUIMenu() {
+        //隐藏虚拟按键，并且全屏
+        if (Build.VERSION.SDK_INT > 11 && Build.VERSION.SDK_INT < 19) { // lower api
+            View v = this.getWindow().getDecorView();
+            v.setSystemUiVisibility(View.GONE);
+        } else if (Build.VERSION.SDK_INT >= 19) {
+            //for new api versions.
+            View decorView = getWindow().getDecorView();
+            int uiOptions = View.SYSTEM_UI_FLAG_HIDE_NAVIGATION
+                    | View.SYSTEM_UI_FLAG_IMMERSIVE_STICKY | View.SYSTEM_UI_FLAG_FULLSCREEN;
+            decorView.setSystemUiVisibility(uiOptions);
+        }
+    }
+

+    private void startBackgroundAnim() {

+            public void onAnimationUpdate(ValueAnimator animation) {
+                int color = (int) animation.getAnimatedValue();

+    private void setupComplete() {

+        //replace the second param:Settings.Secure.USER_SETUP_COMPLETE with "user_setup_complete"

+		//setupDefaultLauncher();
+		Log.d("WelcomeActivity", "dhq setupComplete ");
+    }

+private void setupDefaultLauncher() {  
+        // remove this activity from the package manager.  
+        PackageManager pm = this.getPackageManager();  
+  
+        String examplePackageName = "com.tct.launcher"; //package name
+        String exampleActivityName = "com.tct.launcher.Launcher"; //name
+  
+        ComponentName defaultLauncher = null;  
+  
+        Intent intent = new Intent(Intent.ACTION_MAIN);  
+        intent.addCategory(Intent.CATEGORY_HOME);  
+  
+        List<ResolveInfo> resolveInfoList =  
+                pm.queryIntentActivities(intent, 0);  
+        if (resolveInfoList != null) {  
+            int size = resolveInfoList.size();  
+            for (int j = 0; j < size; ) {  
+                final ResolveInfo r = resolveInfoList.get(j);  
+                if (!r.activityInfo.packageName.equals(examplePackageName)) {  
+                    resolveInfoList.remove(j);  
+                    size -= 1;  
+                } else {  
+                    j++;  
+                }  
+            }  
+            ComponentName[] set = new ComponentName[size];  
+            defaultLauncher = new ComponentName(examplePackageName, exampleActivityName);  
+            int defaultMatch = 0;  
+            for (int i = 0; i < size; i++) {  
+                final ResolveInfo resolveInfo =  
+                        resolveInfoList.get(i);  
+                Log.d(TAG, resolveInfo.toString());  
+                set[i] = new  
+                        ComponentName(resolveInfo.activityInfo.packageName, resolveInfo.activityInfo.name);  
+                if (defaultLauncher.getClassName().equals(resolveInfo.activityInfo.name)) {  
+                    defaultMatch = resolveInfo.match;  
+                }  
+            }  
+            Log.d(TAG, "defaultMatch =" + Integer.toHexString(defaultMatch));  
+            IntentFilter filter = new IntentFilter();  
+            filter.addAction(Intent.ACTION_MAIN);  
+            filter.addCategory(Intent.CATEGORY_HOME);  
+            filter.addCategory(Intent.CATEGORY_DEFAULT);  
+  
+            pm.clearPackagePreferredActivities(defaultLauncher.getPackageName());  
+            pm.addPreferredActivity(filter, defaultMatch, set, defaultLauncher);  
+        }  
+    }
+	
+    private void finishBootWizard() {
+        try {
+
+            PackageManager pm = getPackageManager();
+            ComponentName name = new ComponentName(this, WelcomeActivity.class);
+            pm.setComponentEnabledSetting(name, PackageManager.COMPONENT_ENABLED_STATE_DISABLED, PackageManager.DONT_KILL_APP);
+			Log.d("WelcomeActivity", "dhq finishBootWizard ");
+        } catch (Exception e) {
+            Log.e(TAG, "finishBootWizard: " + e.getMessage());
+        } finally {
+            finishAffinity();
+        }
+    }
+
+
+
+    private boolean isFirstShown() {
+        // TODO: 2017/6/23
+        Intent intent_language = getIntent();
+        boolean fromlanguage = intent_language.getBooleanExtra("fromlanguage", false);
+        return !mIsLastPage && !fromlanguage && !mHasInstance;
+    }
+
+    private int[] getFrameResIds(String pre, int num) {
+        final int[] resIds = new int[num];
+        Resources res = getResources();
+        final String packageName = getPackageName();
+        for (int i = 0; i < resIds.length; i++) {
+            int imageResId = res.getIdentifier(pre + (i + 1), "drawable", packageName);
+            resIds[i] = imageResId;
+        }
+        return resIds;
+    }
+
+    @Override
+    protected void onSaveInstanceState(Bundle outState) {
+        outState.putBoolean(TAG, true);
+//        if (animRecycle != null) {
+//            outState.putInt(CURRENT_LOGO_INDEX, animRecycle.getCurrentIndex());
+//            Log.d(TAG, "onSaveInstanceState: ###logo=" + animRecycle.getCurrentIndex());
+//        }
+        if (animRecycle != null) {
+            outState.putInt(CURRENT_RECYCLE_INDEX, animRecycle.getCurrentIndex());
+            Log.d(TAG, "onSaveInstanceState: ###load");
+        }
+        super.onSaveInstanceState(outState);
+    }

+        Intent intentAction2 = new Intent();
+        intentAction2.setPackage("com.android.systemui");
+        intentAction2.setAction("hide_navigationbar");
+        sendBroadcast(intentAction2);
+    }

+    private int getSavedLanguage() {
+        final Configuration config = getResources().getConfiguration();
+        final Locale locale = config.locale;
+
+        if (Locale.SIMPLIFIED_CHINESE.equals(locale)) return 0;
+        else if (Locale.US.equals(locale)) return 1;
+        else return 2;
+    }
+
+    private void initViewState() {
+        switch (mIndex) {
+            case 1://english
+                webView.loadUrl("file:///android_asset/Gome_Privacy_Policy_US.html");
+                break;
+            case 0://chinese
+                webView.loadUrl("file:///android_asset/Gome_Privacy_Policy_CN.html");
+                break;
+            case 2:
+            default:
+                webView.loadUrl("file:///android_asset/Gome_Privacy_Policy_CN.html");
+                break;
+        }
+    }
+
+    @Override
+    protected void onResume() {
+        super.onResume();

+    private int[] getFrameResIds(String pre, int num) {
+        final int[] resIds = new int[num];
+        Resources res = getResources();
+        final String packageName = getPackageName();
+        for (int i = 0; i < resIds.length; i++) {
+            int imageResId = res.getIdentifier(pre + (i + 1), "drawable", packageName);
+            resIds[i] = imageResId;
+        }
+        return resIds;
+    }

+package com.gome.bootwizard.util;
+
+/**
+ * Created by Administrator on 2017/7/27.
+ */
+
+import java.util.ArrayList;
+
+
+import android.app.Activity;
+import android.app.Application;
+
+public class MyApplication extends Application {
+    private static MyApplication instance;
+    public static ArrayList<Activity> activityList ;
+    private MyApplication() {
+        activityList = new ArrayList<Activity>();
+    }
+
+    /**
+     * 单例模式中获取唯一的MyApplication实例
+     *
+     * @return
+     */
+    public static MyApplication getInstance() {
+        if (null == instance) {
+            instance = new MyApplication();
+        }
+        return instance;
+
+    }
+
+    // 添加Activity到容器中
+    public void addActivity(Activity activity) {
+        if (activityList != null && activityList.size() > 0) {
+            if(!activityList.contains(activity)){
+                activityList.add(activity);
+            }
+        }else{
+            activityList.add(activity);
+        }
+
+    }
+
+    // 遍历所有Activity并finish
+    public void exit() {
+        if (activityList != null && activityList.size() > 0) {
+            for (Activity activity : activityList) {
+                activity.finish();
+            }
+        }
+        activityList.clear();
+//        System.exit(0);
+    }
+    public static void exitApp(){
+
+
+        for (Activity ac : activityList) {
+            if(!ac.isFinishing()){
+                ac.finish();
+            }
+        }
+        activityList.clear();
+       // android.os.Process.killProcess(android.os.Process.myPid());
+    }
+    public static void removeAppActivity(Activity activity){
+        if(activityList.contains(activity)){
+            activityList.remove(activity);
+        }
+    }
+
+
+}

--- vendor/mediatek/proprietary/packages/apps/BootWizard/src/com/gome/bootwizard/util/FrameAnimation.java	(revision 0)

+package com.gome.bootwizard.util;
+
+import android.widget.ImageView;
+
+@SuppressWarnings({"WeakerAccess", "unused"})
+public class FrameAnimation {
+
+    private boolean mIsRepeat;
+    private AnimationListener mAnimationListener;
+    private ImageView mImageView;
+    private int[] mFrameResId;
+    private int[] mDurations;
+    private int mDuration;
+    private int mDelay;
+    private int mLastFrame;
+    private boolean mNext;
+
+    public FrameAnimation(ImageView iv, int[] resId, int duration, boolean isRepeat) {
+        mImageView = iv;
+        mFrameResId = resId;
+        mDuration = duration;
+        mLastFrame = resId.length - 1;
+        mIsRepeat = isRepeat;
+    }
+
+    public FrameAnimation(ImageView iv, int[] resId, int[] durations, boolean isRepeat) {
+        mImageView = iv;
+        mFrameResId = resId;
+        mDurations = durations;
+        mLastFrame = resId.length - 1;
+        mIsRepeat = isRepeat;
+    }
+
+    public FrameAnimation(ImageView iv, int[] resId, int duration) {
+        mImageView = iv;
+        mFrameResId = resId;
+        mDuration = duration;
+        mLastFrame = resId.length - 1;
+    }
+
+    public FrameAnimation(ImageView iv, int[] resId, int[] durations) {
+        mImageView = iv;
+        mFrameResId = resId;
+        mDurations = durations;
+        mLastFrame = resId.length - 1;
+    }
+
+    public void start() {
+        if (mDurations != null) {
+            startPlayByDurations();
+        } else {
+            play(0);
+        }
+    }
+
+    public void startDelay(int delay) {
+        mDelay = delay;
+        if (mDurations != null) {
+            startDelayByDurations(delay);
+        } else {
+            playAndDelay(0);
+        }
+    }
+
+    private void startPlayByDurations() {
+        playByDurations(0);
+    }
+
+    private void startDelayByDurations(int delay) {
+        mDelay = delay;
+        playByDurationsAndDelay(0);
+    }
+
+    private void playByDurationsAndDelay(final int i) {
+        mImageView.postDelayed(new Runnable() {
+
+            @Override
+            public void run() {
+                if (0 == i) {
+                    if (mAnimationListener != null) {
+                        mAnimationListener.onAnimationStart();
+                    }
+                }
+                mImageView.setBackgroundResource(mFrameResId[i]);
+                if (i == mLastFrame) {
+                    if (mAnimationListener != null) {
+                        mAnimationListener.onAnimationRepeat();
+                    }
+                    mNext = true;
+                    playByDurationsAndDelay(0);
+                } else {
+                    playByDurationsAndDelay(i + 1);
+                }
+            }
+        }, mNext && mDelay > 0 ? mDelay : mDurations[i]);
+    }
+
+    private void playAndDelay(final int i) {
+        mImageView.postDelayed(new Runnable() {
+
+            @Override
+            public void run() {
+                mNext = false;
+                if (0 == i) {
+                    if (mAnimationListener != null) {
+                        mAnimationListener.onAnimationStart();
+                    }
+                }
+                mImageView.setBackgroundResource(mFrameResId[i]);
+                if (i == mLastFrame) {
+                    if (mIsRepeat) {
+                        if (mAnimationListener != null) {
+                            mAnimationListener.onAnimationRepeat();
+                        }
+                        mNext = true;
+                        playAndDelay(0);
+                    }
+                } else {
+                    playAndDelay(i + 1);
+                }
+            }
+        }, mNext && mDelay > 0 ? mDelay : mDuration);
+
+    }
+
+    private void playByDurations(final int i) {
+        mImageView.postDelayed(new Runnable() {
+
+            @Override
+            public void run() {
+                if (0 == i) {
+                    if (mAnimationListener != null) {
+                        mAnimationListener.onAnimationStart();
+                    }
+                }
+                mImageView.setBackgroundResource(mFrameResId[i]);
+                if (i == mLastFrame) {
+                    if (mIsRepeat) {
+                        if (mAnimationListener != null) {
+                            mAnimationListener.onAnimationRepeat();
+                        }
+                        playByDurations(0);
+                    } else {
+                        if (mAnimationListener != null) {
+                            mAnimationListener.onAnimationEnd();
+                        }
+                    }
+                } else {
+                    playByDurations(i + 1);
+                }
+            }
+        }, mDurations[i]);
+
+    }
+
+    private void play(final int i) {
+        mImageView.postDelayed(new Runnable() {
+
+            @Override
+            public void run() {
+                if (0 == i) {
+                    if (mAnimationListener != null) {
+                        mAnimationListener.onAnimationStart();
+                    }
+                }
+                mImageView.setBackgroundResource(mFrameResId[i]);
+                if (i == mLastFrame) {
+                    if (mIsRepeat) {
+                        if (mAnimationListener != null) {
+                            mAnimationListener.onAnimationRepeat();
+                        }
+                        play(0);
+                    } else {
+                        if (mAnimationListener != null) {
+                            mAnimationListener.onAnimationEnd();
+                        }
+                    }
+
+                } else {
+                    play(i + 1);
+                }
+            }
+        }, mDuration);
+    }
+
+    public interface AnimationListener {
+
+        void onAnimationStart();
+
+        void onAnimationEnd();
+
+        void onAnimationRepeat();
+    }
+
+    public void setAnimationListener(AnimationListener listener) {
+        this.mAnimationListener = listener;
+    }

+package com.gome.bootwizard.util;
+
+import android.widget.ImageView;
+
+@SuppressWarnings({"WeakerAccess", "unused"})
+public class FrameAnimation2 {
+
+    private boolean mIsRepeat;
+    private AnimationListener mAnimationListener;
+    private ImageView mImageView;
+    private int[] mFrameResId;
+    private int[] mDurations;
+    private int mDuration;
+    private int mDelay;
+    private int mLastFrame;
+    private boolean mNext;
+    private int mIndex;
+
+    public FrameAnimation2(ImageView iv, int[] resId, int duration, boolean isRepeat) {
+        mImageView = iv;
+        mFrameResId = resId;
+        mDuration = duration;
+        mLastFrame = resId.length - 1;
+        mIsRepeat = isRepeat;
+    }
+
+    public FrameAnimation2(ImageView iv, int[] resId, int[] durations, boolean isRepeat) {
+        mImageView = iv;
+        mFrameResId = resId;
+        mDurations = durations;
+        mLastFrame = resId.length - 1;
+        mIsRepeat = isRepeat;
+    }
+
+    public FrameAnimation2(ImageView iv, int[] resId, int duration) {
+        mImageView = iv;
+        mFrameResId = resId;
+        mDuration = duration;
+        mLastFrame = resId.length - 1;
+    }
+
+    public FrameAnimation2(ImageView iv, int[] resId, int[] durations) {
+        mImageView = iv;
+        mFrameResId = resId;
+        mDurations = durations;
+        mLastFrame = resId.length - 1;
+    }
+
+    public void start() {
+        if (mDurations != null) {
+            startPlayByDurations();
+        } else {
+            play(mIndex);
+        }
+    }
+
+    public void startDelay(int delay) {
+        mDelay = delay;
+        if (mDurations != null) {
+            startDelayByDurations(delay);
+        } else {
+            playAndDelay(mIndex);
+        }
+    }
+
+    private void startPlayByDurations() {
+        playByDurations(mIndex);
+    }
+
+    private void startDelayByDurations(int delay) {
+        mDelay = delay;
+        playByDurationsAndDelay(mIndex);
+    }
+
+    private void playByDurationsAndDelay(final int i) {
+        mIndex = i;
+        mImageView.postDelayed(new Runnable() {
+
+            @Override
+            public void run() {
+                if (0 == i) {
+                    if (mAnimationListener != null) {
+                        mAnimationListener.onAnimationStart();
+                    }
+                }
+                mImageView.setBackgroundResource(mFrameResId[i]);
+                if (i == mLastFrame) {
+                    if (mAnimationListener != null) {
+                        mAnimationListener.onAnimationRepeat();
+                    }
+                    mNext = true;
+                    playByDurationsAndDelay(0);
+                } else {
+                    playByDurationsAndDelay(i + 1);
+                }
+            }
+        }, mNext && mDelay > 0 ? mDelay : mDurations[i]);
+    }
+
+    private void playAndDelay(final int i) {
+        mIndex = i;
+        mImageView.postDelayed(new Runnable() {
+
+            @Override
+            public void run() {
+                mNext = false;
+                if (0 == i) {
+                    if (mAnimationListener != null) {
+                        mAnimationListener.onAnimationStart();
+                    }
+                }
+                mImageView.setBackgroundResource(mFrameResId[i]);
+                if (i == mLastFrame) {
+                    if (mIsRepeat) {
+                        if (mAnimationListener != null) {
+                            mAnimationListener.onAnimationRepeat();
+                        }
+                        mNext = true;
+                        playAndDelay(0);
+                    }
+                } else {
+                    playAndDelay(i + 1);
+                }
+            }
+        }, mNext && mDelay > 0 ? mDelay : mDuration);
+
+    }
+
+    private void playByDurations(final int i) {
+        mIndex = i;
+        mImageView.postDelayed(new Runnable() {
+
+            @Override
+            public void run() {
+                if (0 == i) {
+                    if (mAnimationListener != null) {
+                        mAnimationListener.onAnimationStart();
+                    }
+                }
+                mImageView.setBackgroundResource(mFrameResId[i]);
+                if (i == mLastFrame) {
+                    if (mIsRepeat) {
+                        if (mAnimationListener != null) {
+                            mAnimationListener.onAnimationRepeat();
+                        }
+                        playByDurations(0);
+                    } else {
+                        if (mAnimationListener != null) {
+                            mAnimationListener.onAnimationEnd();
+                        }
+                    }
+                } else {
+                    playByDurations(i + 1);
+                }
+            }
+        }, mDurations[i]);
+
+    }
+
+    private void play(final int i) {
+        mIndex = i;
+        mImageView.postDelayed(new Runnable() {
+
+            @Override
+            public void run() {
+                if (0 == i) {
+                    if (mAnimationListener != null) {
+                        mAnimationListener.onAnimationStart();
+                    }
+                }
+                mImageView.setBackgroundResource(mFrameResId[i]);
+                if (i == mLastFrame) {
+                    if (mIsRepeat) {
+                        if (mAnimationListener != null) {
+                            mAnimationListener.onAnimationRepeat();
+                        }
+                        play(0);
+                    } else {
+                        if (mAnimationListener != null) {
+                            mAnimationListener.onAnimationEnd();
+                        }
+                    }
+
+                } else {
+                    play(i + 1);
+                }
+            }
+        }, mDuration);
+    }
+
+    public interface AnimationListener {
+
+        void onAnimationStart();
+
+        void onAnimationEnd();
+
+        void onAnimationRepeat();
+    }
+
+    public void setAnimationListener(AnimationListener listener) {
+        this.mAnimationListener = listener;
+    }
+
+    public int getCurrentIndex() {
+        return mIndex;
+    }
+
+    public void setCurrentIndex(int index) {
+        mIndex = index;
+    }
+}

+package com.gome.bootwizard.util;
+
+import android.content.Context;
+import android.location.LocationManager;
+import android.net.ConnectivityManager;
+import android.net.NetworkInfo;
+import android.telephony.TelephonyManager;
+import android.util.DisplayMetrics;
+
+import java.util.List;
+
+import static android.content.Context.TELEPHONY_SERVICE;
+
+/**
+ * Created by Administrator on 2017/8/21.
+ */
+
+public class WifiUtils {
+    public static boolean isConnect(Context context) {
+        ConnectivityManager manager= (ConnectivityManager) context.getSystemService(Context.CONNECTIVITY_SERVICE);
+        NetworkInfo networkInfo= manager.getActiveNetworkInfo();
+        return networkInfo!=null&&networkInfo.isAvailable();
+    }
+    public static boolean isGpsEnabled(Context context) {
+        LocationManager lm = ((LocationManager) context
+                .getSystemService(Context.LOCATION_SERVICE));
+        List<String> accessibleProviders = lm.getProviders(true);
+        return accessibleProviders != null && accessibleProviders.size() > 0;
+    }
+    public static boolean isMobileEnabled(Context context) {
+        ConnectivityManager cm = (ConnectivityManager) context
+                .getSystemService(Context.CONNECTIVITY_SERVICE);
+        NetworkInfo networkINfo = cm.getActiveNetworkInfo();
+        if (networkINfo != null
+                && networkINfo.getType() == ConnectivityManager.TYPE_MOBILE) {
+            return true;
+        }
+        return false;
+    }
+    public static boolean isNetwork(Context context) {
+        TelephonyManager tm = (TelephonyManager) context.getSystemService(TELEPHONY_SERVICE);
+        int networkType = tm.getNetworkType();
+        int phoneType = tm.getPhoneType();
+        if (TelephonyManager.NETWORK_TYPE_UNKNOWN==networkType&&TelephonyManager.PHONE_TYPE_NONE==phoneType){
+            return false;
+        }else {
+            return true;
+        }
+    }
+
+
+}

+package com.gome.bootwizard.util;
+
+import android.content.Context;
+import android.telephony.TelephonyManager;
+
+/**
+ * This is simple utility to check sim card state.
+ *
+ * @author Yusong.Liang
+ * @date 2017/5/9.
+ */
+public class SIMCardUtils {
+
+    /**
+     * check current sim card state
+     *
+     * @param context {@link Context} object
+     * @return true if sim card is ready,false otherwise
+     */
+    public static boolean isSIMCardReady(Context context) {
+        TelephonyManager telManager = (TelephonyManager) context.getSystemService(Context.TELEPHONY_SERVICE);
+        if (telManager != null) {
+            final int simState = telManager.getSimState();
+            switch (simState) {
+                case TelephonyManager.SIM_STATE_READY:
+                    return true;
+                case TelephonyManager.SIM_STATE_UNKNOWN:
+                case TelephonyManager.SIM_STATE_ABSENT:
+                case TelephonyManager.SIM_STATE_PIN_REQUIRED:
+                case TelephonyManager.SIM_STATE_PUK_REQUIRED:
+                case TelephonyManager.SIM_STATE_NETWORK_LOCKED:
+                default:
+                    return false;
+            }
+        }
+        return false;
+    }
+}

+            Intent intent = new Intent();

+package com.gome.bootwizard.service;
+
+import android.app.KeyguardManager;
+import android.app.Service;
+import android.content.BroadcastReceiver;
+import android.content.Context;
+import android.content.Intent;
+import android.content.IntentFilter;
+import android.os.IBinder;
+
+
+import com.gome.bootwizard.R;
+
+/**
+ * Created by Administrator on 2017/9/20.
+ */
+
+public class ScreenOffService extends Service {
+    @Override
+    public IBinder onBind(Intent intent) {
+        return null;
+    }
+
+    @Override
+    public void onCreate() {
+         IntentFilter filter = new IntentFilter();
+        filter.addAction(Intent.ACTION_SCREEN_OFF);
+        filter.addAction(Intent.ACTION_SCREEN_ON);
+        filter.addAction(Intent.ACTION_USER_PRESENT);
+        registerReceiver(testReceiver, filter);
+        super.onCreate();
+    }
+    public BroadcastReceiver testReceiver = new BroadcastReceiver() {
+        @Override
+        public void onReceive(Context context, Intent intent) {
+            final String action = intent.getAction();
+            if (Intent.ACTION_USER_PRESENT.equals(action)) {
+                hideHomeRecent();
+            }else if (Intent.ACTION_SCREEN_ON.equals(action) && !hasSecurity(context)){
+                hideHomeRecent();
+            }
+        }
+    };
+    private void hideHomeRecent(){
+        Intent intentAction = new Intent();
+        intentAction.setPackage("com.android.systemui");
+        intentAction.setAction("show_navigationbar");
+        sendBroadcast(intentAction);
+//        Intent intentAction = new Intent();
+//        intentAction.setPackage("com.android.systemui");
+//        intentAction.setAction("action_show_back");
+//        sendBroadcast(intentAction);
+        Intent  intentAction3 =  new Intent();
+        intentAction3.setPackage("com.android.systemui");
+        intentAction3.setAction("action_hide_recent");
+        sendBroadcast(intentAction3);
+        Intent  intentAction2 =  new Intent();
+        intentAction2.setPackage("com.android.systemui");
+        intentAction2.setAction("action_hide_home");
+        sendBroadcast(intentAction2);
+    }
+    public static boolean hasSecurity( Context context) {
+
+        KeyguardManager km = (KeyguardManager) context.getSystemService(Context.KEYGUARD_SERVICE);
+        boolean keyguardSecure = km.isKeyguardSecure();
+        return keyguardSecure;
+    }
+    private void hideNavigation(){
+        Intent intentAction2 = new Intent();
+        intentAction2.setPackage("com.android.systemui");
+        intentAction2.setAction("hide_navigationbar");
+        sendBroadcast(intentAction2);
+    }
+
+    @Override
+    public void onDestroy() {
+        super.onDestroy();
+        unregisterReceiver(testReceiver);
+    }
+}

+package com.gome.bootwizard.service;
+
+import java.lang.reflect.Method;
+
+import android.app.Service;
+import android.content.Intent;

+import android.database.Cursor;

+import android.os.Handler;
+import android.os.IBinder;
+import android.provider.CallLog;
+import android.telephony.PhoneStateListener;
+import android.telephony.TelephonyManager;
+
+import com.android.internal.telephony.ITelephony;
+
+public class CallFirewallService extends Service {
+	public static final String TAG = "CallFirewallService";
+	private TelephonyManager tm;
+	private MyPhoneListener listener;
+	@Override
+	public IBinder onBind(Intent intent) {
+		return null;
+	}
+
+
+	@Override
+	public void onCreate() {
+		super.onCreate();
+		listener = new MyPhoneListener();
+		tm = (TelephonyManager) getSystemService(TELEPHONY_SERVICE);
+		tm.listen(listener, PhoneStateListener.LISTEN_CALL_STATE);
+
+	}
+
+	private class MyPhoneListener extends PhoneStateListener {
+		@Override
+		public void onCallStateChanged(int state, String incomingNumber) {
+			switch (state) {
+			case TelephonyManager.CALL_STATE_RINGING:
+					endcall();
+				break;
+			case TelephonyManager.CALL_STATE_IDLE:
+				break;
+			case TelephonyManager.CALL_STATE_OFFHOOK:
+				break;
+			}
+			super.onCallStateChanged(state, incomingNumber);
+		}
+
+	}
+
+
+	@Override
+	public void onDestroy() {
+		super.onDestroy();
+		tm.listen(listener, PhoneStateListener.LISTEN_NONE);
+		listener = null;
+		
+	}
+
+
+	public void endcall() {
+		try {
+			Method method = Class.forName("android.os.ServiceManager")
+					.getMethod("getService", String.class);
+			IBinder binder = (IBinder) method.invoke(null,
+					new Object[] { TELEPHONY_SERVICE });
+			ITelephony telephony = ITelephony.Stub.asInterface(binder);
+			telephony.endCall();
+
+		} catch (Exception e) {
+			e.printStackTrace();
+		}
+	}

+package com.gome.bootwizard.timer;
+
+
+
+import java.util.Date;
+import java.util.Timer;
+import java.util.TimerTask;
+
+
+public class MybTimeTask extends TimerTask{
+
+    private Timer timer = null;
+    private static boolean flag = false;
+
+    private static MybTimeTask mybTimeTask = null;
+    private OnTimerStateChangeListener mOnStateChangeListener;
+    private MybTimeTask(){
+
+    }
+    //单例模式，保持这个对象
+    public static MybTimeTask getInstance(){
+        if (mybTimeTask == null || flag ) {
+            //当flag == true时，为了解决，timer.cancel()后，重新创建一个timer
+            mybTimeTask = new MybTimeTask();
+            if (flag){
+                flag = false;
+            }
+
+        }
+        return mybTimeTask;
+    }
+    public void start(boolean flg) {
+        //毫秒
+        long time = this.getStartTime();
+
+        if (timer == null){
+            timer = new Timer();
+
+        } else {
+            //从此计时器的任务队列中移除所有已取消的任务。
+            timer.purge();
+        }
+
+        timer.scheduleAtFixedRate(this, new Date(), time);
+        System.out.println("定时任务开始...............");
+    }
+
+    public void run() {
+        System.out.println("定时任务执行："+System.currentTimeMillis());  //写自己的逻辑，略
+        if (mOnStateChangeListener != null) {
+            mOnStateChangeListener.run();
+        }
+    }
+
+    public void destroyed(){
+        System.out.println("定时任务销毁............................");
+        //终止此计时器，丢弃所有当前已安排的任务。(不但结束当前schedule，连整个Timer的线程(即当前的定时任务)都会结束掉)
+        timer.cancel();
+        flag = true;
+    }
+
+    private long getStartTime() {
+        //毫秒
+        long i = 100;
+
+        return i;
+    }
+
+
+    public void setTimerStateChangeListener(OnTimerStateChangeListener listener) {
+        mOnStateChangeListener = listener;
+    }
+
+    public interface OnTimerStateChangeListener {
+
+        void run();
+    }
+}

+    }
+

+        TypedArray array = context.obtainStyledAttributes(attrs, R.styleable.AppTitleBar);
+        mNavigationIcon = array.getDrawable(R.styleable.AppTitleBar_navigationIcon);
+        mTitle = array.getString(R.styleable.AppTitleBar_title);
+        mBackgroundColor = array.getColor(R.styleable.AppTitleBar_backgroundColor, 0xFFEFEFF0);
+        array.recycle();
+    }
+
+    private void setupTitleBar() {
+        if (mTitle != null) {
+            tvTitle.setText(mTitle);
+        }
+        if (mNavigationIcon != null) {
+            ibBack.setImageDrawable(mNavigationIcon);
+        }
+        setBackgroundColor(mBackgroundColor);
+    }
+@Override
+	public void onClick(View view) {
+	// TODO Auto-generated method stub
+	switch (view.getId()) {
+		case R.id.ib_title_bar_back:
+		((Activity) getContext()).finish();
+		break;
+	}

+package com.gome.bootwizard.receiver;
+
+import android.app.Service;
+import android.content.BroadcastReceiver;
+import android.content.Context;
+import android.content.Intent;
+import android.telephony.TelephonyManager;
+import android.util.Log;
+
+/**
+ * @author Yusong.Liang
+ * @date 2017/5/10.
+ */
+public class SIMCardStateReceiver extends BroadcastReceiver {
+
+    public final static String ACTION_SIM_STATE_CHANGED = "android.intent.action.SIM_STATE_CHANGED";
+
+    private OnSIMCardStateChangeListener mOnStateChangeListener;
+
+    @Override
+    public void onReceive(Context context, Intent intent) {
+        final String action = intent.getAction();
+        if (ACTION_SIM_STATE_CHANGED.equals(action)) {
+            TelephonyManager tm = (TelephonyManager) context.getSystemService(Service.TELEPHONY_SERVICE);
+            if (tm != null) {
+                final int state = tm.getSimState();
+                boolean simCardReady;
+                switch (state) {
+                    case TelephonyManager.SIM_STATE_READY:
+                        simCardReady = true;
+                        break;
+                    case TelephonyManager.SIM_STATE_UNKNOWN:
+                    case TelephonyManager.SIM_STATE_ABSENT:
+                    case TelephonyManager.SIM_STATE_PIN_REQUIRED:
+                    case TelephonyManager.SIM_STATE_PUK_REQUIRED:
+                    case TelephonyManager.SIM_STATE_NETWORK_LOCKED:
+                    default:
+                        simCardReady = false;
+                        break;
+                }
+                if (mOnStateChangeListener != null) {
+                    Log.e("Wizard###!!!", getClass().getSimpleName()+"onReceive:ready? "+simCardReady+", hashCode = "+hashCode());
+                    mOnStateChangeListener.onSIMCardStateChange(simCardReady);
+                }
+            }
+        }
+    }
+
+    public OnSIMCardStateChangeListener getOnSIMCardStateChangeListener() {
+        return mOnStateChangeListener;
+    }
+
+    public void setOnSIMCardStateChangeListener(OnSIMCardStateChangeListener listener) {
+        mOnStateChangeListener = listener;
+    }
+
+    public interface OnSIMCardStateChangeListener {
+
+        void onSIMCardStateChange(boolean isReady);
+    }
+}
